##### **MAP-Law: Coverage-Driven Retrieval Control for Multi-Turn Legal Consultation**
2605.01486v1 by Qinchuan Cheng, Ruixuan Xie, Jiaqi Liu, Xiaoya Yuan, Yuxin Liu

Legal consultation is a high-stakes, knowledge-intensive task that requires agents to identify relevant legal issues, retrieve authoritative support, and determine when evidence is sufficient for a recommendation. Although retrieval-augmented generation has improved grounding in legal question answering, many multi-turn legal agents still rely on fixed retrieval depth or coarse heuristic control. This often leads to either insufficient support for key legal elements or excessive retrieval that increases context burden and weakens answer focus.
  We propose MAP-Law, a coverage-driven framework for retrieval control in multi-turn legal consultation. MAP-Law models consultation as a controlled retrieval process over a joint structured state consisting of issue nodes, legal element nodes, and evidence nodes. After each retrieval round, the agent computes Element Coverage, Evidence Coverage, and Marginal Gain, and uses these signals to decide whether to continue retrieval, redirect the search, or generate the final response. In this way, MAP-Law turns stopping from a fixed hyperparameter into an interpretable and auditable decision aligned with legal argumentative structure.
  Experiments on a self-constructed dataset of 50 cases across eight labor-law scenarios show that MAP-Law with DeepSeek as the action selector achieves an Element Coverage of 0.860 using only 2.9 retrieval rounds and 5.8 evidence pieces on average. Compared with a fixed seven-round baseline, it reduces evidence volume by over 80% and retrieval rounds by 58%. Ablation results further confirm the independent contributions of coverage-driven stopping, joint graph representation, and LLM-based action selection.

摘要：法律諮詢是一項高風險、知識密集的任務，要求代理人識別相關的法律問題、檢索權威支持，並確定何時證據足以支持建議。儘管增強檢索生成改善了法律問題回答的基礎，但許多多輪法律代理仍然依賴固定的檢索深度或粗略的啟發式控制。這通常導致對關鍵法律要素的支持不足，或過度檢索，增加了上下文負擔並削弱了答案的焦點。<lb/>  
我們提出了MAP-Law，一個基於覆蓋率驅動的多輪法律諮詢檢索控制框架。MAP-Law將諮詢建模為一個受控的檢索過程，該過程在由問題節點、法律要素節點和證據節點組成的聯合結構狀態上進行。每次檢索回合後，代理計算要素覆蓋率、證據覆蓋率和邊際增益，並利用這些信號來決定是否繼續檢索、重新導向搜索或生成最終回應。這樣，MAP-Law將停止從固定的超參數轉變為一個可解釋和可審計的決策，與法律論證結構保持一致。<lb/>  
在一個自建的包含八個勞動法場景的50個案例的數據集上進行的實驗顯示，使用DeepSeek作為行動選擇器的MAP-Law在平均僅使用2.9次檢索回合和5.8個證據的情況下，實現了0.860的要素覆蓋率。與固定的七輪基準相比，它將證據量減少了超過80%，檢索回合減少了58%。消融結果進一步確認了覆蓋率驅動停止、聯合圖表示和基於LLM的行動選擇的獨立貢獻。

##### **LIE: LiDAR-only HD Map Construction with Intensity Enhancement via Online Knowledge Distillation**
2605.01478v1 by Kanak Mazumder, Fabian B. Flohr

Online High-Definition (HD) map construction is a key component of autonomous driving. Recent methods rely on multi-view camera images for cost-effective HD map segmentation, but cameras lack depth information for accurate scene geometry. In contrast, LiDAR provides precise 3D measurements but lacks dense semantic cues. In this work, we propose LIE, LiDAR-only semantic map construction method that employ Knowledge Distillation (KD) to handle the lack of dense semantic and texture cues. Specifically, the teacher branch fuses student LiDAR features and the corresponding 2D intensity map tile to provide dense supervision for segmenting map elements using online distillation scheme. Experimental results show that our method outperforms all single-modality approaches, achieving 8.2% higher mIoU than the state-of-the-art camera-based model on nuScenes. LIE is robust over long ranges and under challenging weather and lighting, and efficiently adapts to Argoverse2 with only 10% fine-tuning, surpassing camera-based models trained on the full dataset. Source code will be available \href{https://iv.ee.hm.edu/lie/}{here}.

##### **ReMedi: Reasoner for Medical Clinical Prediction**
2605.01474v1 by Yushi Cao, Yiming Chen, Hongchao Jiang, Hung-yi Lee, Robby T. Tan

Predicting future clinical outcomes from electronic health records (EHR) remains challenging due to the complexity and heterogeneity of patient data. LLMs have shown strong potential for such predictive tasks, yet existing approaches mainly focus on enhancing medical knowledge through distillation or RAG while relying on the model's internal ability to interpret contextual information. In this work, we present ReMedi (Reasoner for Medical Clinical Prediction), a framework for improving clinical outcome prediction from EHR. ReMedi generates rationale-answer pairs using a challenging sample regeneration mechanism for complex clinical questions, which leverages ground-truth answers as hints to enhance reasoning for further fine-tuning and preference tuning. ReMedi integrates ground-truth outcome guidance into the preference data construction loop, regenerating rationale-answer variants. By tuning on these rationale-answer pairs, the model improves its predictive performance. ##### **Practical Limits of Autonomous Test Repair: A Multi-Agent Case Study with LLM-Driven Discovery and Self-Correction**
2605.01471v1 by Hyukjoo Lee

Maintaining reliable UI test suites in large-scale enterprise applications is a persistent and costly challenge. We present an industrial case study of a multi-agent autonomous testing system evaluated using anonymized execution data from a production-like enterprise UI testing prototype. The application features several hundred dynamic UI elements per screen. Built on a large language model with LangGraph orchestration, Playwright execution, and a RAG knowledge base, the system evolves from human-directed testing toward High-autonomy feature discovery and test execution: given no explicit test targets, it discovers over 100 testable features across 10 UI screens, dynamically expands coverage by an additional 15--30 features through runtime DOM analysis, and iteratively repairs failing tests without human intervention.
  We analyzed 300 consecutive autonomous execution reports encompassing 636 individual test-case executions across 10 distinct scenario families. The system achieved a 70% repair convergence rate at the scenario-family level, with a mean of 3.4 repair iterations to convergence. However, only 10% of scenario families succeeded on first attempt, 38% of reports failed to produce any executable test artifact, and we documented concrete instances of assertion weakening and test-case deletion used as workaround mechanisms to achieve superficial convergence.
  Our findings show that unrestricted autonomy leads to unstable and often misleading outcomes, while constrained autonomy transforms such systems into operationally viable workflows. Rather than advocating full autonomy, our findings suggest that reliable autonomous testing in enterprise-scale settings requires explicit constraints, validation boundaries, and human oversight to preserve semantic correctness and operational trustworthiness.

摘要：維護大型企業應用程式中的可靠 UI 測試套件是一項持續且昂貴的挑戰。<lb/>我們提出了一個工業案例研究，該研究評估了一個多代理自主測試系統，使用來自類生產環境的企業 UI 測試原型的匿名執行數據。<lb/>該應用程式每個螢幕包含數百個動態 UI 元素。<lb/>該系統基於大型語言模型，結合 LangGraph 協調、Playwright 執行和 RAG 知識庫，從人類指導的測試演變為高自主性的特徵發現和測試執行：在沒有明確測試目標的情況下，它在 10 個 UI 螢幕上發現了超過 100 個可測試的特徵，通過運行時 DOM 分析動態擴展了額外的 15 到 30 個特徵的覆蓋範圍，並在沒有人工干預的情況下迭代修復失敗的測試。<lb/>我們分析了 300 份連續的自主執行報告，涵蓋了 10 個不同場景系列中的 636 個單獨測試案例執行。<lb/>該系統在場景系列層面達到了 70% 的修復收斂率，平均需要 3.4 次修復迭代才能收斂。<lb/>然而，只有 10% 的場景系列在第一次嘗試中成功，38% 的報告未能產生任何可執行的測試工件，我們記錄了具體的斷言削弱和測試案例刪除的實例，這些被用作實現表面收斂的變通機制。<lb/>我們的研究結果顯示，無限制的自主性導致不穩定且常常具有誤導性的結果，而受限的自主性則將這些系統轉變為可操作的工作流程。<lb/>我們的研究結果並不主張完全自主，而是表明在企業規模環境中，可靠的自主測試需要明確的約束、驗證邊界和人類監督，以保持語義正確性和操作可信度。

##### **Rethinking Explanations: Formalizing Contrast in Description Logics**
2605.01442v1 by Yasir Mahmood, Arnab Sharma, Axel-Cyrille Ngonga Ngomo, Balram Tiwari

There has been a growing interest in explaining entailments over description logic (DL) knowledge bases. The existing explanation formalisms focus on justifications to explain true axioms, and abductive reasoning to explain missing axioms in a knowledge base. However, these formalisms only point out the reasoning steps behind a (missing) entailment and lack a user-centered approach as they do not consider an inquirer's needs, level of understanding, or prior knowledge. We propose contrastive explanations, aiming at answering "why an axiom P (fact) is true instead of another axiom Q (foil)" over description logic knowledge bases. The motivation arises from the observation that when a user discovers that P has occurred, they are often surprised because they anticipated the occurrence of another similar event Q. Furthermore, individual explanations for "why P" and "why not Q" are unsatisfactory since a user expects to see the difference between P and Q. In this work, we first present formal foundations of contrasting questions and then define contrastive explanations within description logics. To this end, facts include ABox assertions of the form C(x) for a concept C and individual x. Possible foils for such facts are assertions C(y) (contrasting against an individual y), or D(x) (contrasting against a concept D). Additionally, we explore the properties of contrastive explanations in the DL EL and ALC. We also provide an implementation of our definition and an experimental evaluation on KBs of varying sizes.

摘要：對描述邏輯（DL）知識庫的推論解釋越來越受到關注。現有的解釋形式主義專注於對真實公理的解釋和利用溯因推理來解釋知識庫中缺失的公理。然而，這些形式主義僅指出（缺失）推論背後的推理步驟，並缺乏以用戶為中心的方法，因為它們沒有考慮查詢者的需求、理解水平或先前知識。我們提出對比解釋，旨在回答「為什麼公理 P（事實）是真的，而不是另一個公理 Q（對照）」在描述邏輯知識庫中。這一動機源於觀察到當用戶發現 P 發生時，他們常常感到驚訝，因為他們預期發生的是另一個類似事件 Q。此外，對「為什麼 P」和「為什麼不 Q」的個別解釋並不令人滿意，因為用戶期望看到 P 和 Q 之間的差異。在這項工作中，我們首先提出對比問題的形式基礎，然後在描述邏輯中定義對比解釋。為此，事實包括形式為 C(x) 的 ABox 斷言，其中 C 是一個概念，x 是個體。這類事實的可能對照是斷言 C(y)（與個體 y 對比）或 D(x)（與概念 D 對比）。此外，我們探討了 DL EL 和 ALC 中對比解釋的特性。我們還提供了我們定義的實現以及對不同大小知識庫的實驗評估。

##### **Hallucinations Undermine Trust; Metacognition is a Way Forward**
2605.01428v1 by Gal Yona, Mor Geva, Yossi Matias

Despite significant strides in factual reliability, errors -- often termed hallucinations -- remain a major concern for generative AI, especially as LLMs are increasingly expected to be helpful in more complex or nuanced setups. Yet even in the simplest setting -- factoid question-answering with clear ground truth-frontier models without external tools continue to hallucinate. We argue that most factuality gains in this domain have come from expanding the model's knowledge boundary (encoding more facts) rather than improving awareness of that boundary (distinguishing known from unknown). We conjecture that the latter is inherently difficult: models may lack the discriminative power to perfectly separate truths from errors, creating an unavoidable tradeoff between eliminating hallucinations and preserving utility.
  This tradeoff dissolves under a different framing. If we understand hallucinations as confident errors -- incorrect information delivered without appropriate qualification -- a third path emerges beyond the answer-or-abstain dichotomy: expressing uncertainty. We propose faithful uncertainty: aligning linguistic uncertainty with intrinsic uncertainty. This is one facet of metacognition -- the ability to be aware of one's own uncertainty and to act on it. For direct interaction, acting on uncertainty means communicating it honestly; for agentic systems, it becomes the control layer governing when to search and what to trust. Metacognition is thus essential for LLMs to be both trustworthy and capable; we conclude by highlighting open problems for progress towards this objective.

摘要：儘管在事實可靠性方面取得了重大進展，但錯誤——通常被稱為幻覺——仍然是生成式 AI 的一個主要關注點，特別是隨著 LLMs 在更複雜或微妙的情境中被期望提供幫助。<lb/>然而，即使在最簡單的環境中——事實性問題回答，具有明確真相的前沿模型在沒有外部工具的情況下仍然會出現幻覺。我們認為，在這一領域，大多數事實性增益來自於擴展模型的知識邊界（編碼更多事實），而不是提高對該邊界的認識（區分已知和未知）。<lb/>我們推測後者本質上是困難的：模型可能缺乏完美區分真相與錯誤的辨別能力，造成消除幻覺與保持效用之間不可避免的權衡。<lb/>這種權衡在不同的框架下消失。如果我們將幻覺理解為自信的錯誤——在沒有適當限定的情況下提供的不正確信息——那麼在答案或放棄的二分法之外出現了一條第三條路徑：表達不確定性。我們提出忠實的不確定性：將語言上的不確定性與內在的不確定性對齊。<lb/>這是元認知的一個方面——意識到自己不確定性並據此行動的能力。對於直接互動，根據不確定性行動意味著誠實地傳達它；對於代理系統，它成為控制層，決定何時搜索以及信任什麼。因此，元認知對於 LLMs 既值得信賴又有能力至關重要；我們通過強調朝著這一目標進展的開放問題來結束。

##### **HepScript: A Dual-Use DSL for Human-AI Collaborative Data Analysis Workflows in High-Energy Physics**
2605.01423v1 by Junkun Jiao, Tong Liu, Ke Li, Weimin Song, Yipu Liao, Bolun Zhang, Beijiang Liu, Chang-Zheng Yuan, Yue Sun

The escalating data scale in High-Energy Physics (HEP) fuels a growing aspiration for higher analytical efficiency. While Large Language Models (LLMs) offer a path toward automation via agentic AI, they struggle with complex scientific workflows that require deep domain knowledge and are tightly coupled to experiment-specific codebases. To address this, we introduce a methodology centered on HepScript, a dual-use Domain-Specific Language (DSL) for HEP data analysis workflows. HepScript serves as a shared formal interface, abstracting HEP analysis logic into a constrained syntax that is both intuitive for human experts and reliably generable by AI agents. First developed for the Beijing Spectrometer III (BESIII) experiment, HepScript hides the complexity of the underlying software stack, translating high-level analysis intent into low-level, production-ready code. In our case studies, this abstraction reduces the required human-written code by 93\%. Crucially, HepScript's constrained grammar defines a tractable action space, enabling AI agents to autonomously generate executable specifications for core analysis stages directly from published literature with a 95\% success rate. Our work demonstrates a scalable pathway toward human-AI collaborative systems, where a formally specified DSL acts as an unambiguous translation layer between human expertise, AI automation, and production environment, rendering previously intractable automation problems solvable.

摘要：隨著高能物理（HEP）數據規模的擴大，對更高分析效率的渴望也在增長。雖然大型語言模型（LLMs）提供了一條通往通過自主AI實現自動化的道路，但它們在需要深厚領域知識並且與特定實驗代碼庫緊密耦合的複雜科學工作流程中卻面臨挑戰。為了解決這個問題，我們介紹了一種以HepScript為中心的方法論，這是一種用於HEP數據分析工作流程的雙重用途領域專用語言（DSL）。HepScript作為一個共享的正式接口，將HEP分析邏輯抽象為一種受限語法，對人類專家來說直觀，並且可以由AI代理可靠地生成。HepScript最初是為北京光譜儀III（BESIII）實驗開發的，它隱藏了底層軟件堆棧的複雜性，將高層次的分析意圖轉換為低層次、可生產的代碼。在我們的案例研究中，這種抽象將所需的人類編寫代碼減少了93%。至關重要的是，HepScript的受限語法定義了一個可處理的行動空間，使AI代理能夠自主地從已發表的文獻中生成核心分析階段的可執行規範，成功率達到95%。我們的工作展示了一條可擴展的途徑，朝著人類與AI協作系統的方向發展，其中一個正式指定的DSL作為人類專業知識、AI自動化和生產環境之間的明確翻譯層，使得以前難以處理的自動化問題變得可解決。

##### **TimeTok: Granularity-Controllable Time-Series Generation via Hierarchical Tokenization**
2605.01418v1 by Seokhyun Lee, Jaeho Kim, Changjun Oh, Mihaela van der Schaar, Changhee Lee

Time-series generative models often lack control over temporal granularity, forcing users to accept whatever granularity the model produces. To enable truly user-driven generation, we introduce TimeTok, a unified framework for Granularity-Controllable Time-Series Generation (GC-TSG), which generates time series at any target granularity from any coarser input (e.g., rough sketches) or from scratch. At the core of TimeTok is a hierarchical tokenization strategy that maps time series into an ordered sequence of tokens, from coarse to fine temporal granularity. Our autoregressive generation process operates across these granularity levels, producing token blocks that are decoded back into continuous time series. This design naturally enables GC-TSG - including standard generation - within a single framework, where controlling the number of token blocks provides explicit control over output detail. Experiments show that TimeTok excels at GC-TSG tasks while achieving state-of-the-art performance in standard generation. Furthermore, we showcase TimeTok's potential as a foundational tokenizer by training on multiple datasets with heterogeneous temporal granularities, verifying strong transferability that consistently outperforms models trained on individual datasets. To our knowledge, this is the first unified framework that covers the full generative spectrum for time series, offering a valuable foundation for models that benefit from diverse temporal granularities.

摘要：時間序列生成模型通常缺乏對時間粒度的控制，迫使使用者接受模型所產生的任何粒度。為了實現真正以使用者為驅動的生成，我們引入了 TimeTok，一個統一的框架，用於粒度可控的時間序列生成（GC-TSG），它可以從任何粗略的輸入（例如粗略草圖）或從零開始生成任意目標粒度的時間序列。TimeTok 的核心是一種層次化的標記策略，將時間序列映射為一個有序的標記序列，從粗到細的時間粒度。我們的自回歸生成過程在這些粒度層級上運作，生成的標記塊被解碼回連續的時間序列。這一設計自然地在單一框架內實現了 GC-TSG，包括標準生成，其中控制標記塊的數量提供了對輸出細節的明確控制。實驗顯示，TimeTok 在 GC-TSG 任務中表現優異，同時在標準生成中達到了最先進的性能。此外，我們展示了 TimeTok 作為基礎標記器的潛力，通過在多個具有異質時間粒度的數據集上進行訓練，驗證了其強大的可轉移性，並始終超越在單一數據集上訓練的模型。據我們所知，這是第一個涵蓋時間序列生成全範圍的統一框架，為受益於多樣時間粒度的模型提供了有價值的基礎。

##### **AMSnet-q: Unsupervised Circuit Identification and Performance Labeling for AMS Circuits**
2605.01404v1 by Ze Zhang, Junzhuo Zhou, Yichen Shi, Zhuofu Tao, Rui Ji, Zhiping Yu, Quan Chen, Ting-Jung Lin, Lei He

Analog and mixed-signal (AMS) circuit design remains heavily reliant on expert knowledge. While recent AI-driven automation tools can generate candidate topologies, they critically depend on manually curated datasets with functional and performance annotations -- a requirement that current large language models (LLMs) and vision models cannot automate. Existing approaches still require domain experts to manually interpret circuit functionality.
  We present AMSnet-q, a fully automated, unsupervised pipeline that eliminates human-in-the-loop annotation by converting schematic images directly into a labeled AMS circuit database. Unlike prior work that stops at netlist extraction, our framework automates the complete verification loop: it performs schematic-to-netlist conversion, topology-aware testbench generation, and simulation-based sizing validation to objectively determine circuit functionality. Validated in 28 nm technology, AMSnet-q processed 739 schematics from the AMSnet 1.0 dataset, automatically constructing a repository of 4 circuit classes, 105 distinct topologies, and 89,789 labeled device configurations. By decoupling human effort from dataset volume and reducing the workload to a one-time testbench template per circuit class, AMSnet-q enables scalable, objective, and fully automated AMS database construction.

摘要：類比和混合信號（AMS）電路設計仍然高度依賴專家知識。雖然最近的AI驅動自動化工具可以生成候選拓撲，但它們嚴重依賴於手動整理的數據集，這些數據集具有功能和性能註釋——這是當前大型語言模型（LLMs）和視覺模型無法自動化的要求。現有的方法仍然需要領域專家手動解釋電路功能。<lb/>  
我們提出了AMSnet-q，這是一個完全自動化的無監督管道，通過將原理圖圖像直接轉換為標記的AMS電路數據庫，消除了人為註釋的需求。與以往僅停留在網表提取的工作不同，我們的框架自動化了完整的驗證循環：它執行原理圖到網表的轉換、拓撲感知的測試平台生成，以及基於模擬的尺寸驗證，以客觀地確定電路功能。在28納米技術下進行驗證，AMSnet-q處理了來自AMSnet 1.0數據集的739個原理圖，自動構建了4個電路類別、105個不同拓撲和89,789個標記的設備配置的庫。通過將人力工作與數據集的體量解耦，並將每個電路類別的工作量減少為一次性測試平台模板，AMSnet-q實現了可擴展的、客觀的和完全自動化的AMS數據庫構建。

##### **AI Expert Twin: Capturing Expert Cognition for Human-Centred, Practice-Based Learning**
2605.01401v1 by Annie Yuan, Xiaohua Chen, Kalina Yacef, Judy Kay

Tacit knowledge embedded in expert practice remains difficult to capture, formalise, and scale. While AI-driven educational systems have advanced personalisation, learner modelling, affective support, and self-regulated learning, they less often model the tacit reasoning and context-sensitive judgement that underpin expert practice in practice-based domains. This paper introduces the AI Expert Twin, a cognition-centric framework that models expert knowledge as structured, computable representations of procedural actions, semantic concepts, and decision processes. The framework also considers how value-laden preferences, trade-offs, and uncertainty shape expert judgement in practice. We formalise expert cognition as a three-layer representation and capture knowledge from experts under this model, laying the groundwork for integration into AI-powered educational system. A case study in a cultural heritage workshop demonstrates the feasibility of the approach in a real-world setting. The framework is designed to be transferable across domains such as vocational education and creative industries. By embedding expert heuristics into AI while maintaining transparency and learner agency, the AI Expert Twin offers a novel path towards scalable, practice-based learning and invites further research on ethical, human-centred applications of AI in education.

##### **Using LLMs in Software Design: An Empirical Study of GitHub and A Practitioner Survey**
2605.01392v1 by Yifei Wang, Ruiyin Li, Peng Liang, Yangxiao Cai, Zengyang Li, Mojtaba Shahin, Arif Ali Khan, Qiong Feng

Recent advancements in Large Language Models (LLMs) have demonstrated significant potential across a wide range of software engineering tasks, including software design, an area traditionally regarded as highly dependent on human expertise and judgment. However, there has been little research focusing on how LLMs are used in software design, nor on the associated benefits and drawbacks. This paper aims to bridge this gap by empirically investigating how software developers utilize LLMs in the context of software design. We conduct a mixed-methods study, combining a mining study of 291 developer-ChatGPT conversations shared on GitHub with a survey of 65 software practitioners. Our findings reveal nine distinct categories of design tasks supported by ChatGPT, including architecture design, data model design, and the use of design patterns. We further characterize developer-ChatGPT interactions, showing that developers primarily use ChatGPT for knowledge acquisition and design-related code generation, with most tasks situated at the detailed design level. The study identifies seven key benefits of utilizing LLMs in software design as perceived by developers, such as better technology selection and the early detection of design flaws. We also uncover six limitations, including the generation of overly lengthy and difficult-to-read outputs, the creation of inexecutable or incorrect code, and a heavy reliance on context that can lead to hallucinated results. These findings provide an evidence-based characterization of current LLM use in software design from both open-source and practitioner perspectives, highlighting a tension between perceived benefits and limitations, which lays a foundation for future research and the development of effective techniques and tools to integrate LLMs into software design practices.

摘要：最近在大型語言模型（LLMs）方面的進展顯示出在廣泛的軟體工程任務中具有顯著潛力，包括軟體設計，這一領域傳統上被認為高度依賴人類專業知識和判斷。然而，針對LLMs在軟體設計中使用的研究仍然很少，對於相關的優勢和缺點也缺乏探討。本文旨在通過實證研究填補這一空白，調查軟體開發者在軟體設計背景下如何利用LLMs。我們進行了一項混合方法研究，結合了對291個在GitHub上分享的開發者與ChatGPT對話的挖掘研究，以及對65位軟體從業者的調查。我們的研究結果揭示了ChatGPT支持的九個不同設計任務類別，包括架構設計、數據模型設計和設計模式的使用。我們進一步描述了開發者與ChatGPT的互動，顯示開發者主要使用ChatGPT進行知識獲取和設計相關的代碼生成，大多數任務位於詳細設計層面。該研究確定了開發者認為在軟體設計中利用LLMs的七個主要優勢，例如更好的技術選擇和早期檢測設計缺陷。我們還發現了六個限制，包括生成過長且難以閱讀的輸出、創建不可執行或不正確的代碼，以及對上下文的高度依賴，這可能導致幻覺結果。這些發現從開源和實踐者的角度提供了對當前LLM在軟體設計中使用的基於證據的特徵描述，突顯了感知的優勢與限制之間的緊張關係，為未來的研究以及開發有效的技術和工具以將LLMs整合到軟體設計實踐中奠定了基礎。

##### **MemORAI: Memory Organization and Retrieval via Adaptive Graph Intelligence for LLM Conversational Agents**
2605.01386v1 by Hung Pham Van, Nguyen Manh Hieu, Khang Pham Tran Tuan, Nam Le Hai, Linh Ngo Van, Nguyen Thi Ngoc Diep, Trung Le

Large Language Models (LLMs) lack persistent memory for long-term personalized conversations. Existing graph-based memory systems suffer from information dilution, absent provenance tracking, and uniform retrieval that ignores query context. We introduce MemORAI (Memory Organization and Retrieval via Adaptive Graph Intelligence), a framework that integrates three innovations: selective memory filtering with dual-layer compression to retain user-persona-relevant content, a provenance-enriched multi-relational graph tracking factual origins at the turn level, and query-adaptive subgraph retrieval with Dynamic Weighted PageRank that applies query-conditioned edge weighting. Evaluated on LOCOMO and LongMemEval benchmarks, MemORAI achieves state-of-the-art performance in memory retrieval and personalized response generation, demonstrating that selective storage, enriched representation, and adaptive retrieval are essential for coherent, personalized LLM agents.

摘要：大型語言模型（LLMs）缺乏持久的記憶以進行長期的個性化對話。現有的基於圖形的記憶系統存在信息稀釋、缺乏來源追蹤以及忽略查詢上下文的統一檢索等問題。我們介紹了MemORAI（通過自適應圖智能進行的記憶組織和檢索），這是一個整合了三項創新的框架：選擇性記憶過濾，配合雙層壓縮以保留與用戶角色相關的內容；一個豐富來源的多關係圖，在轉換層級追蹤事實來源；以及查詢自適應子圖檢索，使用動態加權PageRank，應用查詢條件邊權重。在LOCOMO和LongMemEval基準測試中進行評估，MemORAI在記憶檢索和個性化回應生成方面達到了最先進的性能，證明了選擇性存儲、豐富表示和自適應檢索對於連貫的個性化LLM代理是至關重要的。

##### **MTA: Multi-Granular Trajectory Alignment for Large Language Model Distillation**
2605.01374v1 by Pham Khanh Chi, Quoc Phong Dao, Thuat Nguyen, Linh Ngo Van, Trung Le, Thanh Hong Nguyen

Knowledge distillation is a key technique for compressing large language models (LLMs), but most existing methods align representations at fixed layers or token-level outputs, ignoring how representations evolve across depth. As a result, the student is only weakly guided to capture the teacher's internal relational structure during distillation, which limits knowledge transfer. To address this limitation, we propose Multi-Granular Trajectory Alignment (MTA), a framework that aligns teacher and student representations along their layer-wise transformation trajectory. MTA adopts a layer-adaptive strategy: lower layers are aligned at the word level to preserve lexical information, while higher layers operate on phrase-level spans (e.g., noun and verb phrases) to capture compositional semantics. We instantiate this idea through a Dynamic Structural Alignment loss that matches the relative geometry among semantic units within each layer. This design is motivated by empirical findings that Transformer representations become increasingly abstract with depth, and is also consistent with linguistic views in which higher-level meaning emerges through the composition of lower-level lexical units. We further incorporate a Hidden Representation Alignment loss to directly align selected teacher-student layers. Experiments show that MTA consistently outperforms state-of-the-art baselines on standard benchmarks, with ablations confirming the contribution of each component.

摘要：知識蒸餾是一種壓縮大型語言模型（LLMs）的關鍵技術，但大多數現有方法在固定層或標記級輸出上對齊表示，忽略了表示在深度上的演變。因此，學生在蒸餾過程中僅受到微弱的指導以捕捉教師的內部關係結構，這限制了知識轉移。為了解決這一限制，我們提出了多粒度軌跡對齊（MTA），這是一個沿著層級轉換軌跡對齊教師和學生表示的框架。MTA採用層自適應策略：較低層在詞級別對齊以保留詞彙信息，而較高層則在短語級範圍內操作（例如，名詞短語和動詞短語）以捕捉組合語義。我們通過動態結構對齊損失來實現這一想法，該損失匹配每層內語義單元之間的相對幾何。這一設計受到實證研究結果的啟發，該結果顯示Transformer表示隨著深度的增加而變得越來越抽象，並且與語言學觀點一致，即高層次的意義通過低層次詞彙單元的組合而出現。我們進一步納入了一個隱藏表示對齊損失，以直接對齊選定的教師-學生層。實驗顯示，MTA在標準基準上穩定地超越了最先進的基線，消融實驗確認了每個組件的貢獻。

##### **Model-Based Proactive Cost Generation for Learning Safe Policies Offline with Limited Violation Data**
2605.01356v1 by Ruiqi Xue, Lei Yuan, Kainuo Cheng, Jing-Wen Yang, Yang Yu

Learning constraint-satisfying policies from offline data without risky online interaction is crucial for safety-critical decision making. Conventional methods typically learn cost value functions from abundant unsafe samples to define safety boundaries and penalize violations. However, in high-stakes scenarios, risky trial-and-error is infeasible, yielding datasets with few or no unsafe samples. Under this limitation, existing approaches often treat all data as uniformly safe, overlooking safe-but-infeasible states - states that currently satisfy constraints but inevitably violate them within a few steps - leading to deployment failures. Drawing inspiration from the concept of knowledge-data integration, we leverage large language models (LLMs) to incorporate natural language knowledge into the policy to address this challenge. Specifically, we propose PROCO, a model-based offline safe reinforcement learning (RL) framework tailored to datasets largely free of violations. PROCO first learns a dynamics model from offline data and constructs a conservative cost function by grounding natural-language knowledge of unsafe states in LLMs, enabling risk estimation even without observed violations. Using the cost function and learned model, PROCO performs model-based rollouts to synthesize diverse counterfactual unsafe samples, supporting reliable feasibility identification and feasibility-guided policy learning. Across a range of Safety-Gymnasium tasks with exclusively safe or minimally risky training data, PROCO integrates seamlessly with a variety of offline safe RL algorithms and consistently demonstrates reduced constraint violations and improved safety performance compared to both the original methods and other behavior cloning baselines.

摘要：學習從離線數據中獲得滿足約束的策略，而不進行風險在線互動，對於安全關鍵的決策制定至關重要。傳統方法通常從大量不安全的樣本中學習成本值函數，以定義安全邊界並懲罰違規行為。然而，在高風險情境中，風險試錯是不可行的，導致數據集幾乎沒有或沒有不安全樣本。在這一限制下，現有的方法往往將所有數據視為均勻安全，忽視了安全但不可行的狀態——這些狀態目前滿足約束，但在幾步內必然違反它們——導致部署失敗。受到知識-數據整合概念的啟發，我們利用大型語言模型（LLMs）將自然語言知識納入策略，以應對這一挑戰。具體而言，我們提出了PROCO，一種基於模型的離線安全強化學習（RL）框架，專為大多數無違規的數據集量身定制。PROCO首先從離線數據中學習動力學模型，並通過將不安全狀態的自然語言知識嵌入LLMs來構建保守的成本函數，即使在沒有觀察到的違規情況下也能進行風險估計。利用成本函數和學習到的模型，PROCO執行基於模型的展開，以合成多樣的反事實不安全樣本，支持可靠的可行性識別和可行性引導的政策學習。在一系列僅包含安全或最低風險訓練數據的Safety-Gymnasium任務中，PROCO與各種離線安全RL算法無縫整合，並與原始方法及其他行為克隆基準相比，始終顯示出減少約束違規和改善安全性能的效果。

##### **AgriKD: Cross-Architecture Knowledge Distillation for Efficient Leaf Disease Classification**
2605.01355v1 by Minh-Dung Le, Minh-Duc Hoang, Hoang-Vu Truong, Thi-Thu-Hong Phan

Automated leaf disease classification is critical for early disease detection in resource-constrained field environments. Vision Transformers (ViTs) provide strong representation capability by modeling long-range dependencies and inter-class relationships; however, their high computational cost makes them impractical for deployment on edge devices. As a result, existing approaches struggle to effectively transfer these rich representations to lightweight models. This paper introduces AgriKD, a cross-architecture knowledge distillation framework for efficient edge deployment, which transfers knowledge from a Vision Transformer (ViT) teacher to a compact convolutional student model. To bridge the representational gap between Transformer and CNN architectures, the proposed approach integrates multiple distillation objectives at the output, feature, and relational levels, where each objective captures a different aspect of the teacher knowledge. This enables the student model to better preserve and utilize transformer-derived global representations. Experiments on multiple leaf disease datasets show that the distilled student achieves performance comparable to the teacher while significantly improving efficiency, reducing model parameters by approximately 172 times, computational cost by 47.57 times, and inference latency by 18-22 times. Furthermore, the optimized model is deployed across multiple runtime formats, including ONNX, TFLite Float16, and TensorRT FP16, achieving consistent predictive performance with negligible accuracy degradation. Real-world deployment on NVIDIA Jetson edge devices and a mobile application demonstrates reliable real-time inference, highlighting the practicality of AgriKD for AI-powered agricultural applications in resource-constrained environments.

摘要：自動化葉片疾病分類對於在資源有限的田野環境中早期疾病檢測至關重要。視覺Transformer（ViTs）通過建模長距離依賴和類別間關係提供強大的表徵能力；然而，其高計算成本使其在邊緣設備上部署變得不切實際。因此，現有方法在有效地將這些豐富的表徵轉移到輕量級模型方面面臨挑戰。本文介紹了AgriKD，一種用於高效邊緣部署的跨架構知識蒸餾框架，該框架將知識從視覺Transformer（ViT）教師轉移到緊湊的卷積學生模型。為了彌補Transformer和CNN架構之間的表徵差距，所提出的方法在輸出、特徵和關係層面整合了多個蒸餾目標，其中每個目標捕捉教師知識的不同方面。這使得學生模型能夠更好地保留和利用Transformer衍生的全局表徵。在多個葉片疾病數據集上的實驗表明，蒸餾後的學生模型在性能上可與教師相媲美，同時顯著提高了效率，將模型參數減少約172倍，計算成本降低47.57倍，推理延遲減少18-22倍。此外，優化模型在多種運行時格式中部署，包括ONNX、TFLite Float16和TensorRT FP16，實現了一致的預測性能，且準確度下降微乎其微。在NVIDIA Jetson邊緣設備和移動應用上的實際部署展示了可靠的實時推理，突顯了AgriKD在資源有限環境中用於AI驅動農業應用的實用性。

##### **ABox Abduction for Inconsistent Knowledge Bases under Repair Semantics**
2605.01341v1 by Anselm Haak, Patrick Koopmann, Yasir Mahmood, Anni-Yasmin Turhan

Given a knowledge base (KB) with a non-entailed fact, the ABox abduction problem asks for possible extensions of the KB that would entail this fact. This problem has many applications, ranging from diagnosis to explainability and repair. ABox abduction has been well-investigated for consistent KBs and classical semantics, but little is known for the case of inconsistent KBs, which can be caused by erroneous data. In this paper we define suitable notions of abduction in this setting and propose criteria that guide abduction towards "useful" hypotheses. To regain meaningful reasoning in the presence of inconsistencies, we use well-established repair semantics. We provide a comprehensive landscape of the complexity of ABox abduction under repair semantics, treating different variants of the abduction problem for the light-weight description logics DL-Lite and EL_bot.

摘要：給定一個包含非推導事實的知識庫 (KB)，ABox 反推問題要求尋找可能的 KB 擴展，以推導出該事實。這個問題有許多應用，從診斷到解釋性和修復。ABox 反推在一致的 KB 和經典語義下已經得到了充分的研究，但對於不一致的 KB 情況，因為錯誤數據而導致的不一致性，卻知之甚少。在本文中，我們定義了在這種情境下合適的反推概念，並提出指導反推朝向「有用」假設的標準。為了在存在不一致的情況下恢復有意義的推理，我們使用了成熟的修復語義。我們提供了在修復語義下 ABox 反推的複雜性全面概述，處理輕量級描述邏輯 DL-Lite 和 EL_bot 的反推問題的不同變體。

##### **GraphSculptor: Sculpting Pre-training Coreset for Graph Self-supervised Learning**
2605.01310v1 by Chuang Liu, Zelin Yao, Xueqi Ma, Luzhi Wang, Mukun Chen, Pinghua Xu, Wenbin Hu

Graph self-supervised learning typically relies on large-scale unlabeled datasets, heavily inflating computational costs. However, empirical evidence suggests that these datasets contain substantial redundancy-our analysis reveals that uniformly subsampling 50% of graphs retains over 96% of downstream performance. To exploit this redundancy, we introduce GraphSculptor for pre-training coreset construction. Unlike methods dependent on additional training-time signals or limited solely to topological statistics, GraphSculptor provides a label-free solution that constructs coresets via two complementary perspectives: intrinsic structure and contextual semantics. Concretely, structural diversity is quantified using intrinsic graph statistics, yielding a structural feature vector for each graph, while semantic diversity is captured by utilizing a pre-trained language model to encode descriptions generated via graph-to-text. GraphSculptor integrates these signals into a unified metric space and performs cluster-aware selection to preserve joint structural-semantic diversity. We further derive a theoretical bound on the loss gap between coreset and full-data pre-training, offering theoretical motivation for our selection formulation. Extensive experiments demonstrate that GraphSculptor effectively sculpts the dataset: a 10% coreset achieves 99.6% of full-data performance while reducing pre-training time by nearly 90%, offering a scalable solution for data-efficient graph pre-training.

摘要：圖形自我監督學習通常依賴於大規模的無標籤數據集，這大幅提高了計算成本。<lb/>然而，實證證據表明這些數據集包含了大量的冗餘——我們的分析顯示，均勻地子抽樣50%的圖形仍然保留了超過96%的下游性能。<lb/>為了利用這種冗餘，我們引入了GraphSculptor來進行預訓練核心集構建。<lb/>與依賴於額外訓練時間信號或僅限於拓撲統計的方法不同，GraphSculptor提供了一種無標籤的解決方案，通過兩個互補的視角構建核心集：內在結構和上下文語義。<lb/>具體而言，結構多樣性是通過內在圖形統計來量化的，為每個圖形產生一個結構特徵向量，而語義多樣性則是通過利用預訓練的語言模型來編碼通過圖形轉文本生成的描述來捕捉的。<lb/>GraphSculptor將這些信號整合到一個統一的度量空間中，並執行集群感知選擇以保留聯合的結構-語義多樣性。<lb/>我們進一步推導出核心集與全數據預訓練之間損失差距的理論界限，為我們的選擇公式提供了理論動機。<lb/>大量實驗表明，GraphSculptor有效地雕刻了數據集：10%的核心集達到了99.6%的全數據性能，同時將預訓練時間減少了近90%，提供了一種可擴展的數據高效圖形預訓練解決方案。

##### **Valley3: Scaling Omni Foundation Models for E-commerce**

To achieve this, we carefully design a four-stage omni e-commerce continued pre-training pipeline, through which Valley3 progressively acquires audio understanding, cross-modal instruction-following, e-commerce domain knowledge, and long-context reasoning capabilities, ultimately evolving into an omni model for diverse e-commerce scenarios. ##### **GIFT: Guided Fine-Tuning and Transfer for Enhancing Instruction-Tuned Language Models**
2605.01256v1 by Zhiwen Ruan, Yichao Du, Jianjie Zheng, Longyue Wang, Yun Chen, Peng Li, Jinsong Su, Yang Liu, Guanhua Chen

A promising paradigm for adapting instruction-tuned language models is to learn task-specific updates on a pretrained base model and subsequently merge them into the instruction-tuned model. However, existing approaches typically treat the instruction-tuned model as a passive target that is only involved at the final merging stage, without guiding the training process. We propose GIFT (Guided Fine-Tuning and Transfer), a simple and efficient framework that incorporates guidance from the instruction model into task adaptation. GIFT fine-tunes a low-rank adapter on the pretrained base model using confidence signals derived from the instruction-tuned model. The learned adapter is then merged into the instruction-tuned model, yielding task-specialized models that preserve general instruction-following behavior. We evaluate GIFT on mathematical and knowledge-intensive benchmarks across multiple model families and scales. Results show that GIFT consistently outperforms direct fine-tuning and representative transfer-based baselines, while maintaining robust generalization and favorable test-time scaling behavior.

摘要：一個有前景的範式是對指令調整的語言模型進行適應，具體方法是在預訓練的基礎模型上學習任務特定的更新，然後將其合併到指令調整模型中。<lb/>然而，現有的方法通常將指令調整模型視為一個被動的目標，僅在最終合併階段參與，而未能指導訓練過程。<lb/>我們提出了GIFT（Guided Fine-Tuning and Transfer），這是一個簡單而高效的框架，將指令模型的指導融入任務適應中。<lb/>GIFT在預訓練的基礎模型上使用來自指令調整模型的信心信號對低秩適配器進行微調。<lb/>然後，學習到的適配器被合併到指令調整模型中，產生保留一般指令遵循行為的任務專用模型。<lb/>我們在多個模型系列和規模上對數學和知識密集型基準測試進行了GIFT的評估。<lb/>結果顯示，GIFT始終優於直接微調和代表性的基於轉移的基準，同時保持穩健的泛化能力和良好的測試時間擴展行為。

##### **SRA: Span Representation Alignment for Large Language Model Distillation**
2605.01205v1 by Quoc Phong Dao, Hoang Son Nguyen, Pham Khanh Chi, Tung Nguyen, Linh Ngo Van, Nguyen Thi Ngoc Diep, Trung Le

Cross-Tokenizer Knowledge Distillation (CTKD) enables knowledge transfer between a large language model and a smaller student, even when they employ different tokenizers. While existing approaches mainly focus on token-level alignment strategies, which are often brittle and sensitive to discrepancies between tokenizers, we argue that the method of aggregating tokens into more robust representations before distillation is of equal importance. In this paper, we introduce \textbf{SRA} (\textbf{S}pan \textbf{R}epresentation \textbf{A}lignment for Large Language Model Distillation), a novel framework that reframes CTKD through the physical lens of Multi-Particle Dynamical Systems. SRA shifts the fundamental unit of alignment from tokens to robust, tokenizer-agnostic spans. We model each span as a cluster of particles and represent its state by its Center of Mass (CoM) - an attention-weighted average that captures rich semantic information. We leverage the concept of span centers of mass with attention-derived weighting to prioritize the most salient spans. In addition, we employ a geometric regularizer to preserve the structural integrity of the representation space and introduce aligned span logit distillation to enhance knowledge transfer across models. In challenging cross-architecture distillation experiments, SRA consistently and significantly outperforms state-of-the-art CTKD baselines, validating our physically-grounded approach.

摘要：跨標記器知識蒸餾 (CTKD) 使得大型語言模型與較小的學生模型之間能夠進行知識轉移，即使它們使用不同的標記器。雖然現有的方法主要集中在標記級別的對齊策略上，但這些策略往往脆弱且對標記器之間的差異敏感，我們認為在蒸餾之前將標記聚合成更穩健的表示方法同樣重要。在本文中，我們介紹了 \textbf{SRA} (\textbf{S}pan \textbf{R}epresentation \textbf{A}lignment for Large Language Model Distillation)，這是一個通過多粒子動力系統的物理視角重新框架 CTKD 的新穎框架。SRA 將對齊的基本單位從標記轉變為穩健的、與標記器無關的跨度。我們將每個跨度建模為一個粒子集群，並通過其質心 (CoM) 來表示其狀態——這是一種捕捉豐富語義信息的注意力加權平均。我們利用帶有注意力衍生加權的跨度質心概念，以優先考慮最顯著的跨度。此外，我們使用幾何正則化器來保持表示空間的結構完整性，並引入對齊的跨度邏輯蒸餾，以增強跨模型的知識轉移。在具有挑戰性的跨架構蒸餾實驗中，SRA 始終顯著超越最先進的 CTKD 基準，驗證了我們基於物理的方法。

##### **GR-Ben: A General Reasoning Benchmark for Evaluating Process Reward Models**
2605.01203v1 by Zhouhao Sun, Xuan Zhang, Xiao Ding, Bibo Cai, Li Du, Kai Xiong, Xinran Dai, Fei Zhang, weidi tang, Zhiyuan Kan, Yang Zhao, Bing Qin, Ting Liu

Currently, process reward models (PRMs) have exhibited remarkable potential for test-time scaling. Since large language models (LLMs) regularly generate flawed intermediate reasoning steps when tackling a broad spectrum of reasoning and decision-making tasks, PRMs are required to possess capabilities for detecting process-level errors in real-world scenarios. However, existing benchmarks primarily focus on mathematical reasoning, thereby failing to comprehensively evaluate the error detection ability of PRMs across diverse reasoning scenarios. To mitigate this gap, we introduce GR-Ben, a process-level benchmark specifically designed for assessing PRM's performance across two primary reasoning domains (science and logic) and nine subdomains. We conduct extensive experiments on a diverse set of 22 models, encompassing both PRMs and LLMs, and derive two key findings: (1) In domains beyond mathematical reasoning, the error-detection ability of existing PRMs and LLMs is found to be markedly weaker by comparison.(2) In general, PRMs are less adept at identifying knowledge-based errors, whereas LLMs exhibit poorer performance in detecting computational errors.We hope GR-Ben can foster future researches on PRMs for general domains, thereby enhancing the reasoning capabilities of LLMs.

摘要：目前，過程獎勵模型（PRMs）在測試時間擴展方面展現了顯著的潛力。由於大型語言模型（LLMs）在處理廣泛的推理和決策任務時，經常會生成有缺陷的中間推理步驟，因此需要PRMs具備在現實場景中檢測過程級錯誤的能力。然而，現有的基準主要集中於數學推理，因而未能全面評估PRMs在多樣推理場景中的錯誤檢測能力。為了填補這一空白，我們推出了GR-Ben，一個專門設計用於評估PRM在兩個主要推理領域（科學和邏輯）及九個子領域中的表現的過程級基準。我們對22個多樣化模型進行了廣泛實驗，涵蓋了PRMs和LLMs，並得出了兩個關鍵發現：（1）在超出數學推理的領域中，現有PRMs和LLMs的錯誤檢測能力相比之下明顯較弱。（2）一般而言，PRMs在識別基於知識的錯誤方面較不擅長，而LLMs在檢測計算錯誤方面表現較差。我們希望GR-Ben能促進未來對於一般領域PRMs的研究，從而增強LLMs的推理能力。

##### **To Use AI as Dice of Possibilities with Timing Computation**
2605.01134v1 by Jia Li, Vipin Kumar, Rui Zhang

The dominant noun-based modeling paradigm has fundamentally constrained AI development, precluding any adequate representation of the future as an open temporal dimension. This paper introduces a verb-based paradigm, together with precise definitions of \emph{timing computation} and \emph{possibility}, that enables AI to function as an effective instrument for realizing the grammar of our thought.
  Applied to longitudinal EHR data from 3,276 breast cancer patients, the framework empirically demonstrates: (1) automatic discovery of clinically significant patient trajectories, and (2) counterfactual timing deduction. Both results are purely data-driven, require no prior domain knowledge, and, to our knowledge, represent the first such demonstrations in the machine learning literature.

摘要：主導的名詞為基礎的建模範式根本上限制了人工智慧的發展，排除了對未來作為開放時間維度的任何充分表徵。本文介紹了一種基於動詞的範式，以及對\emph{時間計算}和\emph{可能性}的精確定義，使人工智慧能夠作為實現我們思維語法的有效工具。<lb/>應用於3,276名乳腺癌患者的縱向電子健康紀錄數據，該框架實證顯示：(1) 自動發現臨床上重要的患者軌跡，以及(2) 反事實時間推演。這兩個結果完全基於數據，無需先前的領域知識，並且據我們所知，這在機器學習文獻中代表了首次此類的實證。

##### **PERSA: Reinforcement Learning for Professor-Style Personalized Feedback with LLMs**
2605.01123v1 by Ravi Ranjan, Utkarsh Grover, Xiaomin Lin, Agoritsa Polyzou

Large language models (LLMs) can provide automated feedback in educational settings, but aligning an LLMs style with a specific instructors tone while maintaining diagnostic correctness remains challenging. We ask how can we update an LLM for automated feedback generation to align with a target instructors style without sacrificing core knowledge? We study how Reinforcement Learning from Human Feedback (RLHF) can adapt a transformer-based LLM to generate programming feedback that matches a professors grading voice. We introduce PERSA, an RLHF pipeline that combines supervised fine-tuning on professor demonstrations, reward modeling from pairwise preferences, and Proximal Policy Optimization (PPO), while deliberately constraining learning to style-bearing components. Motivated by analyses of transformer internals, PERSA applies parameter efficient fine-tuning. It updates only the top transformer blocks and their feed-forward projections, minimizing global parameter drift while increasing stylistic controllability. We evaluate our proposed approach on three code-feedback benchmarks (APPS, PyFiXV, and CodeReviewQA) using complementary metrics for style alignment and fidelity. Across both Llama-3 and Gemma-2 backbones, PERSA delivers the strongest professor-style transfer while retaining correctness, for example on APPS, it boosts Style Alignment Score (SAC) to 96.2% (from 34.8% for Base) with Correctness Accuracy (CA) up to 100% on Llama-3, and Gemma-2. Overall, PERSA offers a practical route to personalized educational feedback by aligning both what it says (content correctness) and, crucially, how it says it (instructor-like tone and structure).

摘要：大型語言模型（LLMs）可以在教育環境中提供自動化反饋，但在保持診斷正確性的同時，將LLMs的風格與特定教師的語調對齊仍然具有挑戰性。我們詢問如何更新LLM以生成自動化反饋，使其與目標教師的風格對齊，而不犧牲核心知識？我們研究如何通過人類反饋的強化學習（RLHF）來調整基於Transformer的LLM，以生成與教授評分風格相匹配的編程反饋。我們介紹PERSA，一個RLHF管道，結合了對教授示範的監督微調、基於成對偏好的獎勵建模和近端策略優化（PPO），同時故意限制學習於具有風格特徵的組件。受到Transformer內部分析的啟發，PERSA應用參數高效的微調。它僅更新頂部Transformer塊及其前饋投影，最小化全局參數漂移，同時提高風格可控性。我們在三個代碼反饋基準（APPS、PyFiXV和CodeReviewQA）上評估我們提出的方法，使用互補的風格對齊和保真度指標。在Llama-3和Gemma-2骨幹上，PERSA在保持正確性的同時，提供了最強的教授風格轉移，例如在APPS上，它將風格對齊分數（SAC）提高到96.2%（從基礎的34.8%），在Llama-3和Gemma-2上正確性準確度（CA）達到100%。總體而言，PERSA提供了一條實用的個性化教育反饋路徑，通過對齊它所說的內容（內容正確性）以及關鍵的表達方式（類似教師的語調和結構）。

##### **New Bounds for Zarankiewicz Numbers via Reinforced LLM Evolutionary Search**
2605.01120v1 by Jay Bhan, Nicole Nobili, Srinivasan Raghuraman, Patrick Langer

The Zarankiewicz number $\textbf{Z}(m, n, s, t)$ is the maximum number of edges in a bipartite graph $G_{m, n}$ such that there is no complete $K_{s, t}$ bipartite subgraph. We determine for the first time the exact values of three Zarankiewicz numbers: $\textbf{Z}(11, 21, 3, 3)=116$, $\textbf{Z}(11, 22, 3, 3)=121$, and $\textbf{Z}(12, 22, 3, 3)=132$. We further establish lower bounds for 41 more Zarankiewicz numbers, including several that are within one edge of the best known upper bound, and we match the established value in four more closed cases. Our results are obtained using OpenEvolve, an open-source evolutionary algorithm based on Large Language Models (LLMs) that iteratively improves algorithms for generating mathematical constructions by optimizing a reward signal which we tailored for this specific problem. These findings provide new extremal graph constructions and demonstrate the potential of LLM-guided evolutionary search to contribute to mathematical research. In addition to presenting the resulting constructions, we report the generation algorithms produced, describe the relevant implementation details, and provide our computational costs. Our costs are remarkably low, at less than \$30 for each Zarankiewicz parameter combination, showing that LLM-guided evolutionary search can be an inexpensive, reproducible, and accessible tool for discovering new combinatorial constructions.

摘要：Zarankiewicz 數 $\textbf{Z}(m, n, s, t)$ 是一個二部圖 $G_{m, n}$ 中的邊數最大值，滿足不存在完整的 $K_{s, t}$ 二部子圖。 我們首次確定了三個 Zarankiewicz 數的精確值：$\textbf{Z}(11, 21, 3, 3)=116$，$\textbf{Z}(11, 22, 3, 3)=121$，以及 $\textbf{Z}(12, 22, 3, 3)=132$。 我們進一步為 41 個 Zarankiewicz 數建立了下界，其中包括幾個與已知最佳上界相差一條邊的數字，並且在另外四個封閉案例中匹配了已確定的值。 我們的結果是使用 OpenEvolve 獲得的，這是一種基於大型語言模型 (LLMs) 的開源進化算法，通過優化我們為此特定問題量身定制的獎勵信號，迭代改進生成數學結構的算法。 這些發現提供了新的極值圖結構，並展示了 LLM 指導的進化搜索在數學研究中貢獻的潛力。 除了呈現生成的結構外，我們還報告了產生的算法，描述了相關的實施細節，並提供了我們的計算成本。 我們的成本相當低，每個 Zarankiewicz 參數組合的成本不到 30 美元，顯示 LLM 指導的進化搜索可以成為發現新組合結構的一種廉價、可重複且易於獲得的工具。

##### **Towards Multi-Agent Autonomous Reasoning in Hydrodynamics**
2605.01102v1 by Jinpai Zhao, Albert Cerrone, Joannes Westerink, Clint Dawson

Single-agent systems (SAS) have become the default pattern for LLM-driven scientific workflows, but routing planning, tool use, and synthesis through a single context window comes with a well-known cost: as tool specifications and observational traces accumulate, the effective context available for each decision shrinks, and end-to-end reliability suffers. We present a multi-agent system (MAS) prototype for hydrodynamics in which specialized agents are coordinated through a Layer Execution Graph (LEG). A planner agent constructs query-specific execution topologies from natural-language routing heuristics that capture domain knowledge without hard-coding it as rigid control logic; specialist agents operate under strict tool allowlists and occupy complementary data-class roles. Between layers, consolidator agents fuse parallel outputs into concise briefs, and a reporter agent synthesizes the final response, while the runtime logs provenance for every tool invocation to support auditability. All benchmarks, ablations, and stress tests use Claude Sonnet~4.6 as the backbone model for both specialist and general-purpose agents. Evaluated on 37 queries spanning six complexity categories, the prototype achieves 93.6% factual precision with a 100% pass rate. Accuracy remains above 90% across runs from single-threaded to five independent parallel tracks, and under simulated loss of individual data sources the system degrades gracefully, still returning substantive partial answers. Together, these results suggest that planner-guided, graph-structured multi-agent orchestration can meaningfully alleviate the context-saturation bottlenecks that constrain monolithic single-agent architectures.

摘要：單一代理系統（SAS）已成為基於大型語言模型（LLM）的科學工作流程的默認模式，但通過單一上下文窗口進行路由規劃、工具使用和合成帶來了一個眾所周知的成本：隨著工具規格和觀察痕跡的積累，每個決策可用的有效上下文縮小，端到端的可靠性受到影響。我們提出了一個多代理系統（MAS）原型，用於流體力學，其中專門的代理通過層執行圖（LEG）進行協調。一個規劃代理從自然語言路由啟發式中構建查詢特定的執行拓撲，這些啟發式捕捉領域知識，而不將其硬編碼為僵化的控制邏輯；專家代理在嚴格的工具允許清單下運作，並擔任互補數據類別角色。在層之間，整合代理將並行輸出融合成簡明的簡報，而報告代理則合成最終回應，同時運行時記錄每次工具調用的來源以支持可審計性。所有基準測試、消融實驗和壓力測試均使用Claude Sonnet~4.6作為專家和通用代理的基礎模型。在涵蓋六個複雜性類別的37個查詢上進行評估，該原型實現了93.6%的事實精確度，並且通過率為100%。在從單線程到五個獨立平行軌道的運行中，準確率保持在90%以上，在模擬單個數據源丟失的情況下，系統優雅地降級，仍然返回實質性的部分答案。綜合這些結果表明，規劃引導的圖結構多代理協調可以有意義地緩解限制單體單代理架構的上下文飽和瓶頸。

#### Abstracts
##### **Safety and accuracy follow different scaling laws in clinical large language models**
2605.04039v1 by Sebastian Wind, Tri-Thien Nguyen, Jeta Sopa, Mahshad Lotfinia, Sebastian Bickelhaup, Michael Uder, Harald Köstler, Gerhard Wellein, Sven Nebelung, Daniel Truhn, Andreas Maier, Soroosh Tayebi Arasteh

Clinical LLMs are often scaled by increasing model size, context length, retrieval complexity, or inference-time compute, with the implicit expectation that higher accuracy implies safer behavior. This assumption is incomplete in medicine, where a few confident, high-risk, or evidence-contradicting errors can matter more than average benchmark performance. We introduce SaFE-Scale, a framework for measuring how clinical LLM safety changes across model scale, evidence quality, retrieval strategy, context exposure, and inference-time compute. To instantiate this framework, we introduce RadSaFE-200, a Radiology Safety-Focused Evaluation benchmark of 200 multiple-choice questions with clinician-defined clean evidence, conflict evidence, and option-level labels for high-risk error, unsafe answer, and evidence contradiction. We evaluated 34 locally deployed LLMs across six deployment conditions: closed-book prompting (zero-shot), clean evidence, conflict evidence, standard RAG, agentic RAG, and max-context prompting. Clean evidence produced the strongest improvement, increasing mean accuracy from 73.5% to 94.1%, while reducing high-risk error from 12.0% to 2.6%, contradiction from 12.7% to 2.3%, and dangerous overconfidence from 8.0% to 1.6%. Standard RAG and agentic RAG did not reproduce this safety profile: agentic RAG improved accuracy over standard RAG and reduced contradiction, but high-risk error and dangerous overconfidence remained elevated. Max-context prompting increased latency without closing the safety gap, and additional inference-time compute produced only limited gains. Worst-case analysis showed that clinically consequential errors concentrated in a small subset of questions. Clinical LLM safety is therefore not a passive consequence of scaling, but a deployment property shaped by evidence quality, retrieval design, context construction, and collective failure behavior.

摘要：臨床 LLM 通常透過增加模型大小、上下文長度、檢索複雜度或推理時計算來擴展，隱含的期望是更高的準確性意味著更安全的行為。這一假設在醫學中是不完整的，因為少數幾個自信的、高風險的或與證據相矛盾的錯誤可能比平均基準表現更為重要。我們引入了 SaFE-Scale，一個測量臨床 LLM 安全性如何隨著模型規模、證據質量、檢索策略、上下文暴露和推理時計算變化的框架。為了實現這一框架，我們引入了 RadSaFE-200，一個專注於放射學安全評估的基準，包含 200 道多選題，並提供臨床醫生定義的乾淨證據、衝突證據，以及針對高風險錯誤、不安全答案和證據矛盾的選項級標籤。我們在六種部署條件下評估了 34 個本地部署的 LLM：閉卷提示（零樣本）、乾淨證據、衝突證據、標準 RAG、代理 RAG 和最大上下文提示。乾淨證據產生了最強的改進，將平均準確率從 73.5% 提高到 94.1%，同時將高風險錯誤從 12.0% 降低到 2.6%，矛盾從 12.7% 降低到 2.3%，危險的過度自信從 8.0% 降低到 1.6%。標準 RAG 和代理 RAG 並未重現這一安全特徵：代理 RAG 在準確性上超過標準 RAG 並減少了矛盾，但高風險錯誤和危險的過度自信仍然保持在高位。最大上下文提示增加了延遲而未能縮小安全差距，額外的推理時計算僅帶來有限的增益。最壞情況分析顯示，臨床上重要的錯誤集中在少數幾道問題上。因此，臨床 LLM 的安全性並不是擴展的被動結果，而是由證據質量、檢索設計、上下文構建和集體失敗行為所塑造的部署特性。

##### **OpenSeeker-v2: Pushing the Limits of Search Agents with Informative and High-Difficulty Trajectories**
2605.04036v1 by Yuwen Du, Rui Ye, Shuo Tang, Keduan Huang, Xinyu Zhu, Yuzhu Cai, Siheng Chen

Deep search capabilities have become an indispensable competency for frontier Large Language Model (LLM) agents, yet their development remains dominated by industrial giants. The typical industry recipe involves a highly resource-intensive pipeline spanning pre-training, continual pre-training (CPT), supervised fine-tuning (SFT), and reinforcement learning (RL). In this report, we show that when fueled with informative and high-difficulty trajectories, a simple SFT approach could be surprisingly powerful for training frontier search agents. By introducing three simple data synthesis modifications: scaling knowledge graph size for richer exploration, expanding the tool set size for broader functionality, and strict low-step filtering, we establish a stronger baseline. Trained on merely 10.6k data points, our OpenSeeker-v2 achieves state-of-the-art performance across 4 benchmarks (30B-sized agents with ReAct paradigm): 46.0% on BrowseComp, 58.1% on BrowseComp-ZH, 34.6% on Humanity's Last Exam, and 78.0% on xbench, surpassing even Tongyi DeepResearch trained with heavy CPT+SFT+RL pipeline, which achieves 43.4%, 46.7%, 32.9%, and 75.0%, respectively. Notably, OpenSeeker-v2 represents the first state-of-the-art search agent within its model scale and paradigm to be developed by a purely academic team using only SFT. We are excited to open-source the OpenSeeker-v2 model weights and share our simple yet effective findings to make frontier search agent research more accessible to the community.

摘要：深度搜索能力已成為前沿大型語言模型（LLM）代理的不可或缺的能力，但其發展仍然被工業巨頭主導。典型的行業流程涉及一個資源密集的管道，涵蓋預訓練、持續預訓練（CPT）、監督微調（SFT）和強化學習（RL）。在本報告中，我們展示了當使用具有信息性和高難度的軌跡進行訓練時，簡單的SFT方法對於訓練前沿搜索代理可能是意想不到的強大。通過引入三個簡單的數據合成修改：擴大知識圖的大小以實現更豐富的探索、擴大工具集的大小以實現更廣泛的功能，以及嚴格的低步過濾，我們建立了更強的基準。在僅用10.6k數據點進行訓練的情況下，我們的OpenSeeker-v2在四個基準測試中達到了最先進的性能（30B大小的代理，使用ReAct範式）：在BrowseComp上為46.0%、在BrowseComp-ZH上為58.1%、在Humanity's Last Exam上為34.6%、在xbench上為78.0%，甚至超越了使用重型CPT+SFT+RL管道訓練的Tongyi DeepResearch，後者分別達到43.4%、46.7%、32.9%和75.0%。值得注意的是，OpenSeeker-v2代表了在其模型規模和範式內由純學術團隊僅使用SFT開發的第一個最先進搜索代理。我們很高興能夠開源OpenSeeker-v2模型權重，並分享我們簡單而有效的發現，使前沿搜索代理研究對社區更加可及。

##### **Redefining AI Red Teaming in the Agentic Era: From Weeks to Hours**
2605.04019v1 by Raja Sekhar Rao Dheekonda, Will Pearce, Nick Landers

AI systems are entering critical domains like healthcare, finance, and defense, yet remain vulnerable to adversarial attacks. While AI red teaming is a primary defense, current approaches force operators into manual, library-specific workflows. Operators spend weeks hand-crafting workflows - assembling attacks, transforms, and scorers. When results fall short, workflows must be rebuilt. As a result, operators spend more time constructing workflows than probing targets for security and safety vulnerabilities.
  We introduce an AI red teaming agent built on the open-source Dreadnode SDK. The agent creates workflows grounded in 45+ adversarial attacks, 450+ transforms, and 130+ scorers. Operators can probe multi-agent systems, multilingual, and multimodal targets, focusing on what to probe rather than how to implement it.
  We make three contributions: 1. Agentic interface. Operators describe goals in natural language via the Dreadnode TUI (Terminal User Interface). The agent handles attack selection, transform composition, execution, and reporting, letting operators focus on red teaming. Weeks compress to hours. 2. Unified framework. A single framework for probing traditional ML models (adversarial examples) and generative AI systems (jailbreaks), removing the need for separate libraries. 3. Llama Scout case study. We red team Meta Llama Scout and achieve an 85% attack success rate with severity up to 1.0, using zero human-developed code

摘要：AI 系統正在進入醫療、金融和國防等關鍵領域，但仍然容易受到對抗性攻擊的威脅。雖然 AI 紅隊是主要的防禦手段，但當前的方法迫使操作員進入手動、特定於庫的工作流程。操作員花費數週手動製作工作流程 - 組裝攻擊、轉換和評分器。當結果不理想時，工作流程必須重建。因此，操作員花費的時間在構建工作流程上超過了對目標進行安全和安全漏洞探測的時間。<lb/>
我們介紹了一個基於開源 Dreadnode SDK 的 AI 紅隊代理。該代理創建的工作流程基於 45 種以上的對抗性攻擊、450 種以上的轉換和 130 種以上的評分器。操作員可以探測多代理系統、多語言和多模態目標，專注於探測什麼，而不是如何實施。<lb/>
我們做出了三項貢獻：1. 代理界面。操作員通過 Dreadnode TUI（終端用戶界面）以自然語言描述目標。代理處理攻擊選擇、轉換組合、執行和報告，讓操作員專注於紅隊工作。數週的工作壓縮到幾小時。2. 統一框架。一個統一的框架用於探測傳統 ML 模型（對抗性示例）和生成 AI 系統（越獄），消除了對單獨庫的需求。3. Llama Scout 案例研究。我們對 Meta Llama Scout 進行紅隊測試，實現了 85% 的攻擊成功率，嚴重性高達 1.0，使用零人類開發的代碼。

##### **Rethinking Reasoning-Intensive Retrieval: Evaluating and Advancing Retrievers in Agentic Search Systems**
2605.04018v1 by Yilun Zhao, Jinbiao Wei, Tingyu Song, Siyue Zhang, Chen Zhao, Arman Cohan

Reasoning-intensive retrieval aims to surface evidence that supports downstream reasoning rather than merely matching topical similarity. This capability is increasingly important for agentic search systems, where retrievers must provide complementary evidence across iterative search and synthesis. However, existing work remains limited on both evaluation and training: benchmarks such as BRIGHT provide narrow gold sets and evaluate retrievers in isolation, while synthetic training corpora often optimize single-passage relevance rather than evidence portfolio construction. We introduce BRIGHT-Pro, an expert-annotated benchmark that expands each query with multi-aspect gold evidence and evaluates retrievers under both static and agentic search protocols. We further construct RTriever-Synth, an aspect-decomposed synthetic corpus that generates complementary positives and positive-conditioned hard negatives, and use it to LoRA fine-tune RTriever-4B from Qwen3-Embedding-4B. Experiments across lexical, general-purpose, and reasoning-intensive retrievers show that aspect-aware and agentic evaluation expose behaviors hidden by standard metrics, while RTriever-4B substantially improves over its base model.

摘要：推理密集型檢索旨在呈現支持下游推理的證據，而不僅僅是匹配主題相似性。這種能力對於代理搜索系統越來越重要，因為檢索器必須在迭代搜索和綜合中提供互補的證據。然而，現有的研究在評估和訓練方面仍然有限：像 BRIGHT 這樣的基準提供狹窄的黃金集並單獨評估檢索器，而合成訓練語料庫通常優化單一段落的相關性，而非證據組合。我們介紹了 BRIGHT-Pro，一個專家註釋的基準，擴展每個查詢以包含多方面的黃金證據，並在靜態和代理搜索協議下評估檢索器。我們進一步構建了 RTriever-Synth，一個方面分解的合成語料庫，生成互補的正例和以正例為條件的困難負例，並用它來對 Qwen3-Embedding-4B 的 RTriever-4B 進行 LoRA 微調。在詞彙、通用和推理密集型檢索器的實驗中，顯示出方面感知和代理評估揭示了標準指標隱藏的行為，而 RTriever-4B 在其基礎模型上有了顯著的改進。

##### **SymptomAI: Towards a Conversational AI Agent for Everyday Symptom Assessment**
2605.04012v1 by Joseph Breda, Fadi Yousif, Beszel Hawkins, Marinela Cotoi, Miao Liu, Ray Luo, Po-Hsuan Cameron Chen, Mike Schaekermann, Samuel Schmidgall, Xin Liu, Girish Narayanswamy, Samuel Solomon, Maxwell A. Xu, Xiaoran Fan, Longfei Shangguan, Anran Wang, Bhavna Daryani, Buddy Herkenham, Cara Tan, Mark Malhotra, Shwetak Patel, John B. Hernandez, Quang Duong, Yun Liu, Zach Wasson, Dimitrios Antos, Bob Lou, Matthew Thompson, Jonathan Richina, Anupam Pathak, Nichole Young-Lin, Jake Sunshine, Daniel McDuff

Language models excel at diagnostic assessments on currated medical case-studies and vignettes, performing on par with, or better than, clinical professionals. However, existing studies focus on complex scenarios with rich context making it difficult to draw conclusions about how these systems perform for patients reporting symptoms in everyday life. We deployed SymptomAI, a set of conversational AI agents for end-to-end patient interviewing and differential diagnosis (DDx), via the Fitbit app in a study that randomized participants (N=13,917) to interact with five AI agents. This corpus captures diverse communication and a realistic distribution of illnesses from a real world population. A subset of 1,228 participants reported a clinician-provided diagnosis, and 517 of these were further evaluated by a panel of clinicians during over 250 hours of annotation. SymptomAI DDx were significantly more accurate (OR = 2.47, p < 0.001) than those from independent clinicians given the same dialogue in a blinded randomized comparison. Moreover, agentic strategies which conduct a dedicated symptom interview that elicit additional symptom information before providing a diagnosis, perform substantially better than baseline, user-guided conversations (p < 0.001). An auxiliary analysis on 1,509 conversations from a general US population panel validated that these results generalize beyond wearable device users. We used SymptomAI diagnoses as labels for all 13,917 participants to analyze over 500,000 days of wearable metrics across nearly 400 unique conditions. We identified strong associations between acute infections and physiological shifts (e.g., OR > 7 for influenza). While limited by self-reported ground truth, these results demonstrate the benefits of a dedicated and complete symptom interview compared to a user-guided symptom discussion, which is the default of most consumer LLMs.

摘要：語言模型在經過精心挑選的醫療案例研究和小插曲的診斷評估中表現優異，與臨床專業人士的表現相當或更佳。 然而，現有研究集中於具有豐富背景的複雜情境，這使得難以得出這些系統在日常生活中報告症狀的患者中的表現結論。 我們通過Fitbit應用部署了SymptomAI，這是一組用於端到端患者訪談和鑑別診斷（DDx）的對話式AI代理，在一項隨機分配參與者（N=13,917）與五個AI代理互動的研究中進行。 這個語料庫捕捉了多樣的溝通方式和來自現實世界人群的疾病的現實分佈。 1,228名參與者報告了臨床醫生提供的診斷，其中517名在超過250小時的註釋過程中由臨床醫生小組進一步評估。 SymptomAI的DDx在盲法隨機比較中比獨立臨床醫生在相同對話下的診斷準確性顯著更高（OR = 2.47，p < 0.001）。 此外，進行專門症狀訪談以引出額外症狀信息的代理策略，在提供診斷之前，表現明顯優於基線的用戶引導對話（p < 0.001）。 對來自美國一般人群小組的1,509次對話的輔助分析驗證了這些結果超越可穿戴設備使用者的普遍性。 我們使用SymptomAI的診斷作為所有13,917名參與者的標籤，分析了近400種獨特疾病的超過500,000天的可穿戴指標。 我們確定了急性感染與生理變化之間的強關聯（例如，流感的OR > 7）。 雖然受限於自我報告的真實情況，但這些結果顯示了專門且完整的症狀訪談相比於用戶引導的症狀討論的好處，而後者是大多數消費者LLM的默認設定。

##### **Physics-Grounded Multi-Agent Architecture for Traceable, Risk-Aware Human-AI Decision Support in Manufacturing**
2605.04003v1 by Danny Hoang, Ryan Matthiessen, Christopher Miller, Nasir Mannan, Ruby ElKharboutly, David Gorsich, Matthew P. Castanier, Farhad Imani

High-precision CNC machining of free-form aerospace components requires bounded compensations informed by inspection, simulation, and process knowledge. Off-the-shelf large language model (LLM) assistants can generate text, but they do not reliably execute risk-constrained multi-step numerical workflows or provide auditable provenance for high-stakes decisions. We present multi-agent knowledge analysis (MAKA), a human-in-the-loop decision-support architecture that separates intent routing, tools-only quantitative analysis, knowledge graph retrieval, and critic-based verification that enforces physical plausibility, safety bounds, and provenance completeness before recommendations are surfaced for human approval. MAKA is instantiated on a Ti-6Al-4V rotor blade machining testbed by fusing virtual-machining path-tracking error fields, cutting-force and deflection simulations, and scan-based 3D inspection deviation maps from 16 blades. The analysis decomposes deviation into an evidence-linked pathing component, a drift-based wear proxy capturing systematic evolution across parts, a residual systematic compliance term, and a variability proxy for instability-aware escalation. In a three-level tool-orchestration benchmark (single-step through $\geq$3-step stateful sequences), MAKA improves successful tool execution by up to 87.5 percentage points relative to an unstructured single-model interaction pattern with identical tool access. Digital twin what-if studies show MAKA can coordinate traceable compensation candidates that reduce predicted surface deviation from order $10^{-2}$in to approximately $\pm 10^{-3}$in over most of the blade within the simulation environment, providing a pre-deployment verification signal for risk-aware human decision-making.

摘要：高精度的自由形狀航空航天元件的 CNC 加工需要基於檢查、模擬和過程知識的有界補償。現成的大型語言模型 (LLM) 助手可以生成文本，但它們無法可靠地執行受風險約束的多步數值工作流程或為高風險決策提供可審計的來源。我們提出了多代理知識分析 (MAKA)，這是一種人機協作的決策支持架構，將意圖路由、僅限工具的定量分析、知識圖譜檢索和基於評論的驗證分開，該驗證在推薦呈現給人類批准之前強制執行物理合理性、安全邊界和來源完整性。MAKA 在 Ti-6Al-4V 轉子葉片加工測試平台上實現，通過融合虛擬加工路徑跟踪誤差場、切削力和偏轉模擬，以及來自 16 片葉片的基於掃描的 3D 檢查偏差圖。該分析將偏差分解為與證據相關的路徑組件、一個基於漂移的磨損代理，捕捉部件間的系統性演變、一個剩余的系統性合規項，以及一個不穩定性意識的變異性代理。在一個三層工具協調基準測試中（從單步到 $\geq$3 步狀態序列），MAKA 相對於具有相同工具訪問的非結構化單模型交互模式提高了成功工具執行率多達 87.5 個百分點。數位雙胞胎的假設研究顯示，MAKA 可以協調可追蹤的補償候選者，將預測的表面偏差從約 $10^{-2}$in 減少到約 $\pm 10^{-3}$in，涵蓋模擬環境中的大部分葉片，為風險意識的人類決策提供了預部署驗證信號。

##### **EQUITRIAGE: A Fairness Audit of Gender Bias in LLM-Based Emergency Department Triage**
2605.03998v1 by Richard J. Young, Alice M. Matthews

Emergency department triage assigns patients an acuity score that determines treatment priority, and clinical evidence documents persistent gender disparities in human acuity assessment. As hospitals pilot large language models (LLMs) as triage decision support, a critical question is whether these models reproduce or mitigate known biases. We present EQUITRIAGE, a fairness audit of LLM-based ESI assignment evaluating five models (Gemini-3-Flash, Nemotron-3-Super, DeepSeek-V3.1, Mistral-Small-3.2, GPT-4.1-Nano) across 374,275 evaluations on 18,714 MIMIC-IV-ED vignettes under four prompt strategies. Of 9,368 originals, 9,346 are paired with a gender-swapped counterfactual. All five models produced flip rates above a pre-registered 5% threshold (9.9% to 43.8%). Two showed directional female undertriage (DeepSeek F/M 2.15:1, Gemini 1.34:1); two were near-parity; one had high sensitivity with weak male-direction asymmetry. DeepSeek's directional bias coexisted with a low outcome-linked calibration gap (0.013 against MIMIC-IV admission), a Chouldechova-style dissociation between within-group calibration and between-pair counterfactual invariance. Demographic blinding reduced Gemini's flip rate to 0.5%; an age-preserving blind variant left DeepSeek with residual F/M 1.25, implicating age as a residual channel. Chain-of-thought prompting degraded accuracy for all five models. A two-model ablation reveals opposite underlying mechanisms for the same directional phenotype: in Gemini the signal is emergent in the combined name+gender swap, while in DeepSeek the gender token alone carries it. EQUITRIAGE shows that group parity, counterfactual invariance, and gender calibration are distinct fairness properties, that intervention effectiveness is model-dependent, and that per-model counterfactual auditing should precede clinical deployment.

摘要：急診部門的分診為患者分配一個急迫性評分，以決定治療優先順序，而臨床證據記錄了人類急迫性評估中持續存在的性別差異。隨著醫院試行大型語言模型（LLMs）作為分診決策支持，一個關鍵問題是這些模型是否重現或減輕已知的偏見。我們提出了EQUITRIAGE，這是一項基於LLM的ESI分配的公平性審核，評估了五個模型（Gemini-3-Flash、Nemotron-3-Super、DeepSeek-V3.1、Mistral-Small-3.2、GPT-4.1-Nano）在18,714個MIMIC-IV-ED小品上的374,275次評估，使用四種提示策略。在9,368個原始樣本中，9,346個與性別交換的反事實配對。所有五個模型的翻轉率均超過預先登記的5%閾值（9.9%至43.8%）。兩個模型顯示出女性的低分診（DeepSeek F/M 2.15:1，Gemini 1.34:1）；兩個模型接近平等；一個模型具有高靈敏度但性別方向不對稱。DeepSeek的方向性偏見與低結果相關的校準差距（對MIMIC-IV入院的0.013）共存，這表明了組內校準與組間反事實不變性之間的Chouldechova風格的解離。人口統計盲測將Gemini的翻轉率降低至0.5%；一個保留年齡的盲變體使DeepSeek的殘餘F/M為1.25，暗示年齡作為一個殘餘通道。鏈式思考提示降低了所有五個模型的準確性。兩模型消融揭示了相同方向表型的相反潛在機制：在Gemini中，信號在結合的名字+性別交換中出現，而在DeepSeek中，僅性別標記就攜帶了它。EQUITRIAGE顯示，群體平等、反事實不變性和性別校準是不同的公平性屬性，干預效果依賴於模型，且每個模型的反事實審核應在臨床部署之前進行。

##### **From Intent to Execution: Composing Agentic Workflows with Agent Recommendation**
2605.03986v1 by Kishan Athrey, Ramin Pishehvar, Brian Riordan, Mahesh Viswanathan

Multi-Agent Systems (MAS) built using AI agents fulfill a variety of user intents that may be used to design and build a family of related applications. However, the creation of such MAS currently involves manual composition of the plan, manual selection of appropriate agents, and manual creation of execution graphs. This paper introduces a framework for the automated creation of multi-agent systems which replaces multiple manual steps with an automated framework. The proposed framework consists of software modules and a workflow to orchestrate the requisite task- specific application. The modules include: an LLM-derived planner, a set of tasks described in natural language, a dynamic call graph, an orchestrator for map agents to tasks, and an agent recommender that finds the most suitable agent(s) from local and global agent registries. The agent recommender uses a two-stage information retrieval (IR) system comprising a fast retriever and an LLM-based re-ranker. We implemented a series of experiments exploring the choice of embedders, re- rankers, agent description enrichment, and supervising critique agent. We benchmarked this system end-to-end, evaluating the combination of planning, agent selection, and task completion, with our proposed approach. Our experimental results show that our approach outperforms the state-of-the- art in terms of the recall rate and is more robust and scalable compared to previous approaches. The critique agent holistically reevaluates both agent and tool recommendations against the overall plan. We show that the inclusion of the critique agent further enhances the recall score, proving that the comprehensive review and revision of task-based agent selection is an essential step in building end-to-end multi-agent systems.

摘要：多智能體系統（MAS）使用 AI 智能體來滿足各種用戶意圖，這些意圖可用於設計和構建一系列相關應用程序。 然而，目前創建這樣的 MAS 涉及手動編排計劃、手動選擇適當的智能體以及手動創建執行圖。 本文介紹了一個自動創建多智能體系統的框架，該框架用自動化框架取代了多個手動步驟。 提議的框架由軟件模塊和工作流程組成，以協調所需的任務特定應用。 模塊包括：一個基於 LLM 的規劃器、一組用自然語言描述的任務、一個動態調用圖、一個將智能體映射到任務的協調器，以及一個從本地和全球智能體註冊表中找到最合適智能體的智能體推薦系統。 智能體推薦系統使用一個由快速檢索器和基於 LLM 的重新排名器組成的兩階段信息檢索（IR）系統。 我們實施了一系列實驗，探討嵌入器、重新排名器、智能體描述增強和監督評估智能體的選擇。 我們對該系統進行了端到端的基準測試，評估了計劃、智能體選擇和任務完成的組合，並與我們提出的方法進行比較。 我們的實驗結果表明，我們的方法在召回率方面優於最先進技術，並且相比於以往的方法更具穩健性和可擴展性。 評估智能體從整體計劃的角度全面重新評估智能體和工具的推薦。 我們展示了評估智能體的納入進一步提高了召回分數，證明了基於任務的智能體選擇的全面審查和修訂是構建端到端多智能體系統的重要步驟。

##### **Flow Sampling: Learning to Sample from Unnormalized Densities via Denoising Conditional Processes**
2605.03984v1 by Aaron Havens, Brian Karrer, Neta Shaul

Sampling from unnormalized densities is analogous to the generative modeling problem, but the target distribution is defined by a known energy function instead of data samples. Because evaluating the energy function is often costly, a primary challenge is to learn an efficient sampler. We introduce Flow Sampling, a framework built on diffusion models and flow matching for the data-free setting. Our training objective is conditioned on a noise sample and regresses onto a denoising diffusion drift constructed from the energy function. In contrast, diffusion models' objective is conditioned on a data sample and regresses onto a noising diffusion drift. We utilize the interpolant process to minimize the number of energy function evaluations during training, resulting in an efficient and scalable method for sampling unnormalized densities. Furthermore, our formulation naturally extends to Riemannian manifolds, enabling diffusion-based sampling in geometries beyond Euclidean space. We derive a closed-form formula for the conditional drift on constant curvature manifolds, including hyperspheres and hyperbolic spaces. We evaluate Flow Sampling on synthetic energy benchmarks, small peptides, large-scale amortized molecular conformer generation, and distributions supported on the sphere, demonstrating strong empirical performance.

摘要：從未標準化密度進行抽樣類似於生成建模問題，但目標分佈是由已知的能量函數定義，而不是數據樣本。因為評估能量函數通常是昂貴的，所以主要挑戰是學習一個高效的抽樣器。我們介紹了流抽樣（Flow Sampling），這是一個基於擴散模型和流匹配的框架，適用於無數據的情境。我們的訓練目標是以噪聲樣本為條件，並回歸到由能量函數構建的去噪擴散漂移。相對而言，擴散模型的目標是以數據樣本為條件，並回歸到加噪擴散漂移。我們利用插值過程來最小化訓練期間能量函數評估的次數，從而實現一種高效且可擴展的方法來抽樣未標準化的密度。此外，我們的公式自然擴展到黎曼流形，使得在超越歐幾里得空間的幾何中進行基於擴散的抽樣成為可能。我們推導了常曲率流形上條件漂移的閉合形式公式，包括超球面和雙曲空間。我們在合成能量基準、小肽、大規模攤銷分子構象生成以及支持在球面上的分佈上評估了流抽樣，展示了強大的實證性能。

##### **Logical Consistency as a Bridge: Improving LLM Hallucination Detection via Label Constraint Modeling between Responses and Self-Judgments**
2605.03971v1 by Hao Mi, Qiang Sheng, Shaofei Wang, Beizhe Hu, Yifan Sun, Zhengjia Wang, Hengqi Zeng, Yang Li, Danding Wang, Juan Cao

Large Language Models (LLMs) are prone to factual hallucinations, risking their reliability in real-world applications. Existing hallucination detectors mainly extract micro-level intrinsic patterns for uncertainty quantification or elicit macro-level self-judgments through verbalized prompts. However, these methods address only a single facet of the hallucination, focusing either on implicit neural uncertainty or explicit symbolic reasoning, thereby treating these inherently coupled behaviors in isolation and failing to exploit their interdependence for a holistic view. In this paper, we propose LaaB (Logical Consistency-as-a-Bridge), a framework that bridges neural features and symbolic judgments for hallucination detection. LaaB introduces a "meta-judgment" process to map symbolic labels back into the feature space. By leveraging the inherent logical bridge where response and meta-judgment labels are either the same or opposite based on the self-judgment's semantics, LaaB aligns and integrates dual-view signals via mutual learning and enhances the hallucination detection. Extensive experiments on 4 public datasets, across 4 LLMs, against 8 baselines demonstrate the superiority of LaaB.

摘要：大型語言模型（LLMs）容易出現事實性幻覺，這使其在現實世界應用中的可靠性受到威脅。現有的幻覺檢測器主要提取微觀層面的內在模式以進行不確定性量化，或通過口頭提示引出宏觀層面的自我判斷。然而，這些方法僅解決幻覺的單一面向，專注於隱含的神經不確定性或明確的符號推理，從而將這些本質上相互耦合的行為孤立處理，未能利用其相互依賴性來獲得整體視角。在本文中，我們提出了LaaB（邏輯一致性作為橋樑），這是一個將神經特徵和符號判斷連接起來的幻覺檢測框架。LaaB引入了一個“元判斷”過程，將符號標籤映射回特徵空間。通過利用反應和元判斷標籤在自我判斷語義上相同或相反的內在邏輯橋樑，LaaB通過互學習對齊和整合雙視角信號，並增強幻覺檢測。在4個公共數據集上，針對4個LLMs和8個基準的廣泛實驗展示了LaaB的優越性。

##### **Feature-Augmented Transformers for Robust AI-Text Detection Across Domains and Generators**
2605.03969v1 by Mohamed Mady, Johannes Reschke, Björn Schuller

AI-generated text is nowadays produced at scale across domains and heterogeneous generation pipelines, making robustness to distribution shift a central requirement for supervised binary detectors. We train transformer-based detectors on HC3 PLUS and calibrate a single decision threshold by maximising balanced accuracy on held-out validation; this threshold is then kept fixed for all downstream test distributions, revealing domain- and generator-dependent error asymmetries under shift. We evaluate in-domain on HC3 PLUS, under cross-dataset transfer to the multi-domain, multi-generator M4 benchmark, and on the external AI-Text-Detection-Pile. Although base models achieve near-ceiling in-domain performance (up to 99.5% balanced accuracy), performance under shift is brittle and strongly model-dependent. Feature augmentation via attention-based linguistic feature fusion improves transfer, with our best model (DeBERTa-v3-base+FeatAttn) achieving 85.9% balanced accuracy on M4. Multi-seed experiments confirm high stability. Under the same fixed-threshold protocol, our model outperforms strong zero-shot baselines by up to +7.22 points. Category-level ablations further show that readability and vocabulary features contribute most to robustness under shift. Overall, these results demonstrate that feature augmentation and a modern DeBERTa backbone significantly outperform earlier BERT/RoBERTa models, while the fixed-threshold protocol provides a more realistic and informative assessment of practical detector robustness.

摘要：AI 生成的文本如今在各個領域和異質生成管道中大規模產出，使得對於分佈變化的穩健性成為監督式二元檢測器的一個核心要求。<lb/>我們在 HC3 PLUS 上訓練基於Transformer的檢測器，並通過最大化在保留的驗證集上的平衡準確率來校準單一決策閾值；這個閾值隨後固定於所有下游測試分佈，揭示了在變化下依賴於領域和生成器的錯誤不對稱性。<lb/>我們在 HC3 PLUS 上進行領域內評估，並在跨數據集轉移到多領域、多生成器的 M4 基準上進行評估，以及在外部的 AI-Text-Detection-Pile 上進行評估。<lb/>儘管基礎模型在領域內表現接近上限（高達 99.5% 的平衡準確率），但在變化下的表現脆弱且強烈依賴於模型。<lb/>通過基於注意力的語言特徵融合進行特徵增強改善了轉移，我們的最佳模型（DeBERTa-v3-base+FeatAttn）在 M4 上達到 85.9% 的平衡準確率。<lb/>多種種子實驗確認了高穩定性。<lb/>在相同的固定閾值協議下，我們的模型超越強大的零樣本基準，最多提高 7.22 分。<lb/>類別級的消融進一步顯示可讀性和詞彙特徵對於在變化下的穩健性貢獻最大。<lb/>總體而言，這些結果顯示特徵增強和現代 DeBERTa 主幹顯著超越早期的 BERT/RoBERTa 模型，而固定閾值協議提供了對實際檢測器穩健性更現實和更具信息性的評估。

##### **Label-Efficient School Detection from Aerial Imagery via Weakly Supervised Pretraining and Fine-Tuning**
2605.03968v1 by Zakarya Elmimouni, Fares Fourati, Mohamed-Slim Alouini

Accurate school detection is essential for supporting education initiatives, including infrastructure planning and expanding internet connectivity to underserved areas. However, many regions around the world face challenges due to outdated, incomplete, or unavailable official records. Manual mapping efforts, while valuable, are labor-intensive and lack scalability across large geographic areas. To address this, we propose a weakly supervised framework for school detection from aerial imagery that minimizes the need for human annotations while supporting global mapping efforts. Our method is specifically designed for low-data regimes, where manual annotations are extremely scarce. We introduce an automatic labeling pipeline that leverages sparse location points and semantic segmentation to generate infrastructure masks from which we generate bounding boxes. Using these automatically labeled images, we train our detectors on a first training stage to learn a representation of what schools look like, then using a small set of manually labeled images, we fine-tune the previously trained models on this clean dataset. This two stage training pipeline enables large-scale and strong detection in low-data setting of school infrastructure with minimal supervision.
